<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Third Quarter Highlights</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; October 20, 2010 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc. (NYSE:ACL) reported that global sales rose 9.0 percent to $1.76 billion for the third quarter of 2010.&#160;&#160;Revenue from acquisitions added 70 basis points to sales growth in the quarter, while foreign currency fluctuations reduced reported sales growth by 40 basis points.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Net earnings for the third quarter of 2010 declined 13.4 percent to $446 million, or $1.47 per diluted share, compared to $515 million, or $1.71 per diluted share in the third quarter of 2009.&#160;&#160;Reported net earnings in the third quarter of 2010 include $113 million in after-tax other operating expenses related to the change of majority ownership and merger proposal from Novartis AG.&#160;&#160;Excluding these expenses, non-GAAP adjusted net earnings would have grown 8.5 percent to $559 million, or $1.84 per diluted share, compared to third quarter 2009 net earnings.&#160;&#160;Reconciliations of reported and adjusted results for the third quarter are included in the financial tables below.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;Alcon&#8217;s operational and financial performance in the third quarter clearly demonstrates our ability to combine our commercial capabilities and global scale to achieve sustainable organic growth.&#160;&#160;Once again, we have delivered high-quality results from our core operations, supplemented by strong growth from our recent acquisitions,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s president and chief executive officer.&#160;&#160;&#8220;With the solid results posted in the first three quarters of the year, we are on track to deliver against our full-year revenue and profit guidance.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Sales Highlights</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are sales highlights for the third quarter of 2010. All growth comparisons are for the third quarter of 2010 compared to the third quarter of 2009. Organic sales growth rates exclude currency impacts and acquisitions and are non-GAAP measures that are reconciled in a table at the end of this release.</font></div>

</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Earnings Highlights</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Summarized below are earnings highlights for the third quarter of 2010. All growth comparisons are for the third quarter of 2010 compared to the third quarter of 2009.</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

<td>

</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

</td>
<td>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Operating income declined 14.4 percent to $495 million, or 28.1 percent of sales.&#160;&#160;Non-GAAP adjusted operating income would have increased 8.7 percent to $628 million, or 35.7 percent of sales.&#160;&#160;This performance was attributable to solid sales growth, positive price contribution, the temporary favorable impact of foreign exchange rates on gross profit and SG&amp;A leverage.&#160;&#160;The solid growth in operating profit was achieved while increasing spending on value creating commercial activities and growing R&amp;D spending by over 16 percent.&#160;&#160;Adjusted operating income in the third quarter of 2010 excludes $133 million in other operating expenses related to the change of majority ownership and merger proposal from Novartis.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Financial Guidance</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The company affirmed its full year 2010 guidance for organic sales growth in the high single digits and raised earnings per share guidance to $7.58 to $7.68.&#160;&#160;Guidance includes the impact of higher research and development spending than in the third quarter and the potential for additional business development transactions.&#160;&#160;It also includes the on-going impact of health care reform, which is expected to reduce full year 2010 sales by $20 million and earnings per share by $0.06.&#160;&#160;Guidance excludes costs related to the change of majority ownership to Novartis and the first quarter impact of a change in royalty estimate.&#160;&#160;It also excludes the catch-up impact of the change in tax treatment of U.S. retiree medical expenses related to U.S. health care reform. The full year guidance ass
umes renewal of the U.S. Research and Experimentation tax credit in the fourth quarter of 2010 with retroactive application.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Company Description</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon, Inc. is the world&#8217;s leading eye care company, with sales of approximately $6.5 billion in 2009.&#160; Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic industry for 65 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contacts lens solutions and other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions of the eye.&#160; Alcon operates in 75 countries and sells products in 180 markets.&#160; For more information on Alcon, Inc., visit the Company&#8217;s web site at <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.alcon.com</font>.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Change in constant currency calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations. Management believes constant currency sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note: Change in constant currency calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange fluctuations. Management believes constant currency sales change is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>
